<page sig="a1v">
<section type="title">
<heading>
&para; The <term lang="la">flores</term> of Ouide <term lang="la">de arte amandi</term> with theyr en<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
glysshe afore them: and two alphabete  tablys. The
fyrst begynneth with the englysshe hauyng the laten
wordes folowynge. the other with the laten hauyng <expan type="y+e">the</expan>
englysshe wordes folowynge.
</heading>
</section>
</page>

<page sig="a2r">
<section type="Ovid's distichs">
<wordgroup1 type="u">
<heading>
<term lang="la">Primum distichon.</term>  &para; i: &para; 1.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en"><f type="Bk">S</f>wifte shippis be gouerned be craft / &amp; with seale and oure &amp; a light
swyfte chare is gouerned by crafte: and lyke wyse loue most be go<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
uerned by crafte.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Arte citre / velo<expan type="q3">que</expan> rates / remo<expan type="q3">que</expan> reguntur
Arte leuis currus: arte regendus amor</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Secundum</term>  &para; ii	&para; 2.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">In the beg<expan type="i+_">in</expan>ning first of al labour to fynd it that thu may desyer to loue
for thyn own <expan type=",p">pro</expan>fit the which c<expan type="o+_">om</expan>myst now first a neue soudier <expan type="i+_">in</expan> to harnes</form>
<xpln lang="la">Principio / quod amare velis: reperire labora:
Qui noua nunc primum miles in arma venis.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Tercium</term>	&para; iii.	&para; 3.	
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">An hunter knowith wel where he may <emend err="strechout">strech out</emend> his netis to take har&shy;
tis. and buckys. and he vnderstondith surely: in what valey a fromyng
wylde bere shud tary commynly.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Scit bene venator: ceruis vbi retia tendat.
Scit bene: qua frendens valle moretur aper.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Quartum</term>	&para; iiii.	&para; 4.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Shrubis be knoen to byrders. &amp; he that may t<expan type="e+_">en</expan>th whokys (that is to sey
the fysher) knowith whiche watirs shuld be comyn moche fische.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Aucupibus noti frutices. qui sustinet hamos
Nouit: que multo pisce natentur aque.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Quintum.</term>		&para; v.	&para; 5.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">I wol not c<expan type="o+_">om</expan>maunde the to gyue the seylis to the wyndis rechelesly ta&shy;
kynge noon hede. whan thu sychest for a thyng. ner on the tother partie
ther is no long wey rowgh to be brokyn of the to fynde it.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Non ego querentem ventis dare vela iubebo.
Nec tibi / vt inuenias: longa terenda via est.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Sextum.</term>	&para; vi. 	&para; 6.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en"> Let birdis kepe sil<expan type="e+_">en</expan>s afore ver time: &amp; grashopis afore sumer. let the dog
of the hille menal<expan type="+9">us</expan> (that is to sey the gra<expan type="u+_">un</expan>t or spanyel) sich as be broght
vp there: gyue is back to the hare: takyng no hede of hym afore s<expan type="u+_">um</expan>mer.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Vere prius volucres taceant estate cicade.
Menalius lepori det sua terga canis.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Septimum.</term>		&para; vii.	&para; 7.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">The female /that is to sey the cow /lowith alwey to the bulle in the soft
delicate medows. and the female that is to sey the mare neyth euer to
the horne fotide horse.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Mollibus in pratis admugit femina tauro
Femina cornipedi semper adhinnit equo.</xpln></wordentry>	

<heading>
<term lang="la">Octauum.</term>	&para; viii.	&para; 8.
</heading>
</page>

<page sig="a2v">
<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">The corne is alwey r<expan type="o+_">on</expan>kyr. in other menys fildis: th<expan type="a+_">an</expan> in oure own: as we
thynk. &amp; oure neyghpurs catel hath a grettir vdder than ours.</form>
<xpln lang="la"><term lang="la">Fertilior seges est alienis semper in agris
Vicinum<expan type="q3">que</expan> pecus grandius vber habet.</term></xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Nonum.</term>	&para; ix	&para; 9.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">A chaunce st<expan type="o+_">on</expan>dith in happe. therfore thof som man whyl apply to thyn&shy;
gis of boldnes (wheryn chaunce / or happe st<expan type="o+_">on</expan>dith) yet my counseyl is to
absteyne /or forbere them.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Casus in euentu est. licet hic indulgeat ausis.
Consilium tamen est abstinuisse meum</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Decimum.</term>	&para; x.	&para; 10.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">I wol not goo c<expan type="u+_">um</expan>berly by en hedlyng passage &amp; sharpe rought hilly cly&shy;
fis. <emend err="neryet">ner yet</emend> any body of yong folke shal be bygylid whyle I am is gyde.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Non ego per preceps: &amp; acuta cacumina vadam
Nec iuuen<expan type="u+_">um</expan> quis<expan type="qp+_">quam</expan>. me duce captus erit.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vndecimum.</term>	&para; xi.	&para; 11.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">A byrde scapith not awey prefetably for hym self: whan his wyngis be
lymyd: and lyke whyse a bore gouth not <emend err=".ightly">lightly</emend> out of the nettis: whan
they be let slake.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Non auis vtiliter viscatis effugit alis
Non bene de laxis cassibus exit aper.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Duo decimum.</term>	&para; xii.	&para; 12.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Sede shuld not at euery seson lyke by put or c<expan type="o+_">om</expan>myttyd to the deceuabyl
feldys. ner the holowe shede at all sesons to the grene water.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Non semper credenda ceres fallacibus aruis
Nec semper viridi concaua puppis aque.</xpln></wordentry>		

<heading>
<term lang="la">&para; Terciumdecimum.</term>	&para; xiii.	&para; 13.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">&para; Ten mouthes with euyn so many t<expan type="u+_">un</expan>gis cowd not be enogh for me to
shew pleinly the false forsworne craftis of comyn women.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Non michi sacrilegas meretric<expan type="u+_">um</expan> vt persequar artes:
Cum totidem linguis sint satis ora decem.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Quartumdecimum.</term>		&para; xiiii.	&para; 14.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en"> para; By leyser obstynate yong steris come sobirly ynough to the plough.
like wyse by continuans of tyme horsis be taught to suffer ther brydils
slake.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Tempore difficiles veniunt ad aratra iuuenci.
Tempore lenta pati frena docentur equi.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Quintumdecimum.</term>		&para; xv. &para; 15.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">&para; <emend err="Anharde">An harde</emend> yron rynge is consumyd and wastid awey be continual vse
lycke wyse the holow croked sharre fallith awey with the besey fretyng
erthe.</form>
</page>

<page sig="a3r">
<xpln lang="la">Ferreus assiduo consumitur anulus vsu.
Interit assidua vomer aduncus humo.</xpln></wordentry>	

<heading>
<term lang="la">Sextumdecimum.</term>	&para; xvi.		&para; 16.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">what is more harde than a stone: what thynge is softer than the wattir
yet the herde stonys be made holow with the soft water.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Quid magis est durum saxo? quid mollius est vnda?
Dura tamen molli saxa cauantur aqua</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Septim<expan type="u+_">um</expan>decimum.</term>		&para; xvii.		&para; 17.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Let worfere plese the to vse it: whyle thu arte yong: let thy body be ma&shy;
de dunne with the felde and opyn ayre: care not for the sone brynynge.
but let the gowne be wel sittynge /and clyne wythout ony spot.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Milicie placeant: fuscentur corpora campo.
Sit bene conueniens &amp; sine labe toga</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Decim<expan type="u+_">um</expan>octau<expan type="u+_">um</expan>.</term>		&para; xviii.	&para; 18.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Bothe let thy naylys nothyng apere out langer than thy fynguers: and
let them be clene without filthe vndernethe: &amp; <emend err="it">let</emend> no grete heris stonde
withyn thy holow nose holis.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Et nichil emineant: &amp; sint sine sordibus vngues
Inque caua nullus stet tibi nare pilus.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Decimum nonum.</term>  &para; xix.  	&para; 19.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Let thy mate take al thyngis at the tabyl first yere thu begyn whether
he be of lower degre / or equale with the. nere dout not to speke the se&shy;
cund wordis to hym sufferinge hym to haue the first bothe of the meet /
and wordes: if he wole.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Siue sit inferior / seu par: prior omnia sumat:
Nec dubites vlli verba secunda loqui.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesimum.</term>  &para; xx  &para; 20.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">A certen mesure of drynkynge shall be geuyn / or alowyde the of vs: so
that bothe mynde and fete may fulfill theyr office /or dutye.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Certa tibi a nobis dabitur mensura bibendi
Officium prestent mens<expan type="q3">que</expan> pedes<expan type="q3">que</expan> suum.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesimum prim<expan type="u+_">um</expan>.</term> &para; xxi.  	&para; 21.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Beware of braulyngis /specially prouokyd with wyne / and of hondis
ouer lyght or swifte to wyld cruel batelis.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Iurgia (precipue vino stimulata) caueto:
Et nunium faciles ad fera bella manus.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> secundum.</term> &para; xxii.  	&para; 22.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Like as very dronkynness indede hurtith: euyn so feynede dronkennes
shall helpe / or <expan type=",p">pro</expan>fet otherwhyle therfore cause that thy suttyl deceytfull
tunge that is to sey / that thy tunge whan thu gost about suttiltes: may
st<expan type="u+_">um</expan>bil with a buffynge sonde.</form>
</page>

<page sig="a3v">
<xpln lang="la">Ebrietas vt vera nocet: sic ficta iuuabit.
Fac: titubet bleso subdolet lingua sono.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> tertium.</term> &para; xxiii. 	&para; 23.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Cause that ouer myche wyne may be supposid to abyn the cause therof
watsomeuer thu shalt sey / or do more frowardly than ryght: that is to
sey: than ryght wolle.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Fac quicquid dices: facies<expan type="q3">que</expan> proteruius equo:
Credatur nimium causa fuisse merum.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> quartum.</term> &para; xxiiii. 	&para; 24.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">whyle ther is tyme with vs of comynyng: fle forre hens thu rude vplon<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
dishe shamefastnes: for bothe fortune / &amp; the goddes of loue helpe a bol&shy;
de man.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Colloquii dum tempus abest: fuge rustice longe:
Hinc pudor audacem sors<expan type="q3">que</expan>, Venus<expan type="q3">que</expan> iuuant.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> quintum.</term> &para; xxv. 	&para; 25.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">A feyner of loue slacke at the begynnyng hath oftyntymys in conclusi<expan type="o+_">on</expan>
fal an honde to loue ernestly: &amp; hath byn oftymys it matyr indede after&shy;
warde that he hath feynid hymselfe to be: whan he beganne.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Sepe tepens vere cepit simulator amare.
Sepe<expan type="q3">que</expan> quod incipiens finxerat esse fuit.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> sextum.</term> &para; xxvi. 	&para; 26.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">It is lauful to gete a bodyis mynde priuely by flatteryngis: &amp; so to faul
in fauer with hym. as the hangyng bancke shal com vnder the clere ma<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
tyr: whan hit hath preueyly fretyn awey the erthe vndernethe.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Blanditijs animum furtim deprendere fas est:
Vt pendens liquida ripa subibit aqua.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> septim<expan type="u+_">um</expan></term>	&para; xxvii. 	&para; 27.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Ielde ayen to the owner the pledge: or it that is left with you in kepyin
whan he callith for hit.  Let charetably loue kepe his couenandis. let de<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
ceyt / or gylde be awey fro you. and wholde youre handis voyde gyltles
or hungylty of murther.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Reddite depositum: pietas sua federa seruet:
Fraus absit vacua cedis habete manus.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> octau<expan type="u+_">um</expan>.</term> &para; xxviii.	&para; 28.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Begyle the begylers. &para; For ther is no law more ryghtous th<expan type="a+_">an</expan> that the
craftis men of dethe /or myshefe shulde perishe by theyr owne crafte / &amp;
hondy warke.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Fallite fallentes. &para; Ne<expan type="q3">que</expan> enim lex iustior vlla est.
Quam necis artifices arte perire sua.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Vigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> nonum.</term> &para; xxix. 	&para; 29.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">One maner grounde or countrey bryngest not fourth al maner thyngis
</page>

<page sig="a4r">
for one manere a greyth to viyndis: an other to oylis here in annother
place corne graynys grow wel.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Non tellus eadem parit omnia: vitibus illa.
Conuenit: hec oleis: hic bene farra virent.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesimum.</term> &para; xxx. 	&para; 30.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Therby as many maner condicions in menys brestys / or hartis: as ther
be dyuers figuris in the worlde. therfore he that is wyse shal be apte / or
mete appliynge hym selfe to those vnnumerable maners.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Pectoribus mores tot sunt: quot in orbe figure.
Qui sapit: innumeris moribus aptus erit.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> prim<expan type="u+_">um</expan></term>   &para; xxxi. 	&para; 31.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">One maner gyse of lyuynge shal not agre mete to al thyn yerys of age.
for an olde woman crokyd for age wolle caste for fauce suttiltes farther
than a yonge canne.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Non tibi conueniet cunctos modus vnus ad annos.
Longius insideas curua videbit anus.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> secund<expan type="u+_">um</expan>.</term> &para; xxxii. 	&para; 32.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">wherto <emend err="makyh">makyth</emend> so grete haste y<expan type="o+_">on</expan>ge man: thy shyppe saillith in the mydil
of the watyrs / &amp; the hauyn is forre awey: that I desyre for the.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Quid <expan type=",p">pro</expan>peras iuuenis? medijs tua pinus in vndis
Nauigat. &amp; longe / quem peto: portus abest</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> tercium.</term> &para; xxxiii.	&para; 33.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">It is no lesse vertue to defende or meynteyne thyngis gatte: th<expan type="a+_">an</expan> to gete
them: for there in mayntynynge them stondith chaunce / or fortune &amp; he&shy;
re in getyng them shal be nede of crafte.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Non minor est virtus que querere: parta tueri:
Casus inest illic: hic erit artis opus.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> quart<expan type="u+_">um</expan></term> &para; xxxiiii. 	&para; 34.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Iuyl greuous thyngis meue many witt of tymys to fynde maruels re&shy;
medy for who wold a wende: that euer any man cowd a byn able to ta&shy;
ke the weys of the eyre fleyng / as Dedalus dide.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Ingenium mala sepe mouent. quis crederet vn<expan type="qp+_">quam</expan>:
Aerias hominem carpere posse vias?</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> quint<expan type="u+_">um</expan>.</term> &para; xxxv. 	35.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Let all wronge / or curstnes be forre awey f<emend err="">r</emend>om the / be lauynge and g<expan type="e+_">en</expan>til
that thu mayst be loued thyselfe / the whiche thy beuty / or goodly shape
aloonly shal not gefe the.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Sit procul omne nefas. vt ameris amabilis esto.
Quod tibi non facies: solaue forma dabit</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> sext<expan type="u+_">um</expan></term> &para; xxxvi. 	&para; <emend err="35">36</emend>.
</heading>
</page>

<page sig="a4v">
<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Beuty is a brytyl goodnes. and as myche as / or the more it drawith to
the yeris of age: the lesse it growith yn valure / and it is blamide for his
longe space of the tyme passed.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Forma bon<expan type="u+_">um</expan> fragile est: quant<expan type="u+_">um</expan><expan type="q3">que</expan> accedit ad annos.
Fit minor: &amp; spacio carpitur illa suo.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> septim<expan type="u+_">um</expan>.</term> &para; xxxvii. 	&para; 37.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Neyther the violetis be freshe continualy ner the lilyis floreshe alwey
stil: in there feyre whyte coloure. and lyke wyse the stalke left be hynde
waxid styf / dry / &amp; harde: whan his rose is goon.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Nec semper viole: nec semper lilia florent.
Et riget amissa spina relicta rosa.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> octau<expan type="u+_">um</expan>.</term> &para; xxxviii. 	&para; 38.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">And so lyke wyse feyre childe white heris wol com to the withyn a whil
whan the floris of thy vthe be goon: ther wol also shortly come ryuyls
the whiche wol ere thy body with pletis lyke <emend err="s">f</emend>orows.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Et tibi iam venient cani formose capilli.
Iam venient ruge: que tibi corpus arent.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Trigesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> non<expan type="u+_">um</expan>.</term> &para; xxxix. 	&para; 39.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Tyre now by tyme yn thy vthe / and dresse gay with vertue / and litte&shy;
ral sciens thy mynde: the whiche may dure continualy: &amp; therafter hight
thy bewty. for he (thy minde) bydith stille aloon to the last pangis /or se&shy;
rymonyis of dethe.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Iam molire anim<expan type="u+_">um</expan>: qui duret &amp; astrue formam
Solus ad extremos permanet ille rogas.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">&para; Quadragesimum.</term> &para; xl. 	&para; 40.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">Let not thy diligens be light or retheles to hight thy brest with gentil&shy;
manly literal craftis / and to lerne perfetly tway l<expan type="a+_">an</expan>gages / latyn &amp; greke.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Nec leuis ingenuas pectus coluisse per artes

</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">who wold warne a body to take examplis of gret thynges for his auto<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
rite or defens to the smaller thyngys: and to not drede gretly the name
and: autoritie of a ledar.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Quis vetet a magnis ad res exempla minores
Sumere: nec nomen pertimuisse ducis.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Octuagesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> prim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> prim<expan type="u+_">um</expan>.</term> &para; lxxxi. 	&para; 81.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">we suffer not comynly swet <emend err="pleser ful">pleserful</emend> thyngis beynge c<expan type="o+_">on</expan>tent stille with
them: but we be reneut with the byttyr yuse of cha<expan type="u+_">un</expan>ge abilnes: likewise
the boot many tymys gouth to wrak ouer throw with his own wyndis</form>
<xpln lang="la">Dulcia non ferimus: succo renouamur amaro
Sepe perit ventis obruta cymba suis.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Octuagesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> secund<expan type="u+_">um</expan>:</term> &para; lxxxii. 	&para; 82.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">A lusty stomakyd hors (roshyng out as sone as the stabil is opyn) r<expan type="a+_">an</expan>nith
stoutly then: whan he hath c<expan type="o+_">om</expan>peny: whom he may out goo and whom he
may folow.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Tum bene fortis equus (reserato carcere) currit.
Cum quos pretereat quos<expan type="q3">que</expan> sequatur: habet</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Octuagesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> tercium.</term> &para; lxxxiii.	&para; 83.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">whyther am I brought madde man that I am. why am I synde be myn
own madnes ayenst myn emny with my brest opyn vnharnest: &amp; am be<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
trade myselfe through myn own shewynge: <expan type="p+_">pre</expan>sentynge myself folyshly.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Quo feror insanus: quid a<expan type="p_-">per</expan>to pectore in host<expan type="e+_">em</expan>.
Mittor / &amp; indicio prodor ab ipse meo.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Octuagesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> quartum.</term> &para; lxxxiiii. 	&para; 84.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">A bird shewith not the birders: <expan type="i+_">in</expan> what <expan type="p-_">par</expan>te or coost he shud be sought fore
ner the heynd / or do techeth the spyit <emend err="emni ful">emniful</emend> doggis to r<expan type="a+_">an</expan>ne ap<expan type="o+_">on</expan> hym</form>
<xpln lang="la">Non auis aucupibus monstrat: qua parte petatur
Nec docet infestos currere cerua canes.</xpln></wordentry>

<heading>
<term lang="la">Octuagesim<expan type="u+_">um</expan> quintum.</term> &para; lxxxv.	&para; 85.
</heading>

<wordentry type="h"><form lang="en">It is light / yefe / or esy to bryng about: that shuld wene we were loued
for belefe or feithful trust of optynnyng theyr intend c<expan type="o+_">om</expan>mith anon redy
to couettes folke after theyr desyris.</form>
<xpln lang="la">Effectu facile est: vt nos credamus amari.
Prona venit cupidis in sua vota fides.</xpln></wordentry>

de arte amandi.</term>

<section type="English-Latin lexicon">
<heading>The Englysshe Alphabete</heading>

<f type="bk">T</f>Hese englysshes folowynge haue as many laten wordes after th<expan type="e+_">em</expan>
as be f<expan type="u+_">un</expan>de <expan type="i+_">in</expan> this wark afore hauynge the same englyshe. of whom
they / that be most <expan type=",p">pro</expan>per to the englyshe: st<expan type="o+_">on</expan>de nexte it. &amp; al / that be of the
<expan type="v'">er</expan>sis: begynne with captale letters &amp; they that be not with smale letters.
for we haue added moch englysh more than is laten fore in the versis to
make the sent<expan type="e+_">en</expan>s playn: to whom we haue also addid laten for chyldren:
that they shuld lacke not laten wordis to make theyr englyshe in to lat<expan type="e+_">en</expan>
worde by worde as nygh: as the dyuersite of the langages wol soffer.
<p>

<term lang="la"><f type="Bk">N</f>Ostr<expan type="u+_">um</expan> ex<expan type="e+_">em</expan>plar (vt text<expan type="+9">us</expan> ouidian<expan type="+9">us</expan> <expan type="e+_">est</expan>) <expan type="h3">habet</expan> <expan type="i+_">in</expan>. i. disticho Arte cite vbi cerni<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
tis Arte citre. &amp; <expan type="i+_">in</expan>. 39. ille rogos vbi illa rogas  Si cui anglica ortogra<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
phia non placeat: michi impericie parcat: non det impressorem vicio.  Vt
lingua mutatur: ita &amp; noster calamus.</term>

<section type="Latin-English lexicon">
<heading>Latinum Alphabetum.</heading>

<f type="bk">L<f type="bl">Ike as the Englysshe alphabete afore serueth to gete many laten
wordes for one englysshe/ euyn so douth this lat<expan type="e+_">en</expan> alphabete to gete
many <expan type="e+_">en</expan>glyssh wordes for one lat<expan type="e+_">en</expan> worde of whom the lat<expan type="e+_">en</expan> hath fyrst the
most vside englyssh: as it aperith folowyng in theyr places by these tway
wordes <term lang="la">Bene/ &amp; In.</term> After euery englyssh folowth the nombre shewyng:
where the vses folowyng abbreueat/ may be fo<expan type="u+_">un</expan>d alenth with theyr en&shy;
glyssh/ After <expan type="y+e">the</expan> genityf of subst<expan type="a+_">an</expan>tiues/ <expan type="y+e">the</expan> which shewith <expan type="y+e">the</expan> decl<expan type="e+_">en</expan>son folouth
for <term lang="la">mas. ge. m. fo fem. m.</term> for <term lang="la">neutri n.</term> for c<expan type="o+_">omon</expan>is c. for <term lang="la">dubii d.</term> &amp; for <term lang="la">epiceni e.</term>
Subst<expan type="a+_">an</expan>tiues endyng <expan type="i+_">in</expan> <term lang="la">a</term> be femyn <expan type="i+_">in</expan> <expan type="y+e">the</expan> plu. Lyke wyse
endyng <expan type="i+_">in</expan> <term lang="la">tas</term> be femyn  <expan type="i+_">in</expan> &amp; <expan type="i+_">in</expan> <term lang="la"><expan type="u+_">um</expan></term> neu. therfore we put not letters to shew theyr
g<expan type="e+_">en</expan>der. In <expan type=",p">pro</expan>nownes/ <expan type="p-_">par</expan>tycyples &amp; other adiectyues/ were there be thre ter<emend err="">&shy;</emend>
minacions: <expan type="y+e">the</expan> fyrst is masculyn the mydyl femyn/ &amp; the last neuter. where
therbe twayne the fyrst is of <expan type="y+e">the</expan> comyn g<expan type="e+_">en</expan>der/ &amp; <expan type="y+e">the</expan> later of <expan type="y+e">the</expan> neuter where
there is but one: it is of euery g<expan type="e+_">en</expan>der. In <expan type="v'">ver</expan>bes of <expan type="y+e">the</expan> fyrst c<expan type="o+_">on</expan>iugaci<expan type="o+_">on</expan> kepyng
this forme <term lang="la">O</term> as/ <term lang="la">aui at<expan type="u+_">um</expan></term>. or els <term lang="la">Or aris atuss<expan type="u+_">um</expan></term> we put but <expan type="y+e">the</expan> <expan type="i+_">in</expan>fynityf <expan type="pse+_ r">present</expan>
&amp; so lyke wyse of <expan type="y+e">the</expan> fourth kepyng this forme <term lang="la">Io is iui it<expan type="u+_">um</expan></term>/ or els/ <term lang="la">Ior iris
itus s<expan type="u+_">um</expan></term>. In all other we set out <expan type="y+e">the</expan> fyrst <expan type="p+_">per</expan>sones &amp; the seconde with theyr pre&shy;
tert<expan type="e+_">en</expan>ses/ &amp; supynes yf they be in vse: yf not we put <expan type="y+e">the</expan> infinytyf  present. fo&shy;
lowyng them: that be in vse.
